<p><b>Edgar Steven Davids</b> (<small>Dutch pronunciation:&#32;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Dutch" title="Help:IPA/Dutch">[ˈɛdɡɑr ˈdaːvɪts]</a></span>&#32;<span class="nowrap" style="font-size:85%">(<span class="unicode haudio"><span class="fn"><span style="white-space:nowrap;margin-right:.25em;"><a href="/wiki/File:Nl-Edgar_Davids.ogg" title="About this sound"><img alt="About this sound" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" decoding="async" width="11" height="11" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="20" data-file-height="20" /></a></span><a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/1/1d/Nl-Edgar_Davids.ogg" class="internal" title="Nl-Edgar Davids.ogg">listen</a></span></span>)</span>; born 13 March 1973) is a Dutch-Surinamese former professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a>. After beginning his career with <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>, winning several domestic and international titles, he subsequently played in Italy for <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a>, and later enjoyed a successful spell with <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>, before being loaned out to <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> in 2004. He went on to play for <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> before returning to Ajax. Having struggled with injuries for two years, Davids returned to competitive football during a brief spell with <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a> before retiring at the age of 37. In 2012, he was appointed <a href="/wiki/Player-manager" class="mw-redirect" title="Player-manager">player-manager</a> at the English <a href="/wiki/Football_League_Two" class="mw-redirect" title="Football League Two">League Two</a> club Barnet. He resigned by mutual agreement as manager in January 2014. He was <a href="/wiki/Cap_(sport)" title="Cap (sport)">capped</a> 74 times by the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> at international level, scoring six goals, and represented his country at the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> (once) and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship" title="UEFA European Championship">UEFA European Championship</a> (three times).
</p><p>One of the greatest and most recognisable players of his generation,<sup id="cite_ref-football-oranje.com_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-football-oranje.com-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Davids often stood out on the football field due to his <a href="/wiki/Dreadlocks" title="Dreadlocks">dreadlocked</a> hair and the protective goggles he wore due to <a href="/wiki/Glaucoma" title="Glaucoma">glaucoma</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> A combative and energetic, yet creative and skilful <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfielder</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Defoe_excited_by_Davids_signing_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defoe_excited_by_Davids_signing-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Davids was nicknamed "The Pitbull" by <a href="/wiki/Louis_van_Gaal" title="Louis van Gaal">Louis van Gaal</a> because of his <a href="/wiki/Marking_(association_football)" title="Marking (association football)">marking</a> ability, aggression, and hard tackling style of play.<sup id="cite_ref-tuttojuve.com_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tuttojuve.com-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-One-on-One_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-One-on-One-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Davids:_Dutch_can_go_all_the_way_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Davids:_Dutch_can_go_all_the_way-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> In 2004, he was one of the players chosen by <a href="/wiki/Pel%C3%A9" title="Pelé">Pelé</a> to feature in the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_100" title="FIFA 100">FIFA 100</a>, his list of the world's greatest living footballers.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Early life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Davids was born in <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">Suriname</a> and is of <a href="/wiki/Afro-Surinamese" title="Afro-Surinamese">Afro-Surinamese</a> and partial Jewish descent.<sup id="cite_ref-Parents_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Parents-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> The family moved to the Netherlands when Davids was an infant.<sup id="cite_ref-Parents_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Parents-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> His cousin <a href="/wiki/Lorenzo_Davids" title="Lorenzo Davids">Lorenzo</a> is also a footballer.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ajax">Ajax</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Ajax">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="box-Expand_section plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg" class="image"><img alt="[icon]" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="14" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="44" data-file-height="31" /></a></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs expansion</b>. <small>You can help by <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">adding to it</a>.</small>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">June 2013</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>After being rejected on two previous occasions by the club,<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Davids started his career at the age of 12 with <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He made his first team debut on 6 September 1991 in a 5–1 home win over <a href="/wiki/RKC_Waalwijk" title="RKC Waalwijk">RKC Waalwijk</a>. He helped the <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam" title="Amsterdam">Amsterdam</a> club to three domestic <a href="/wiki/Eredivisie" title="Eredivisie">Eredivisie</a> titles, as well as continental success with the <a href="/wiki/1991%E2%80%9392_UEFA_Cup" title="1991–92 UEFA Cup">1992 UEFA Cup</a> and the <a href="/wiki/1994%E2%80%9395_UEFA_Champions_League" title="1994–95 UEFA Champions League">1995 UEFA Champions League</a>. In the <a href="/wiki/1996_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="1996 UEFA Champions League Final">1996 UEFA Champions League final</a>, he missed Ajax's first <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">shoot-out</a>, which they ultimately lost to <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>. While at Ajax, Davids was nicknamed "The <a href="/wiki/Pit_bull" title="Pit bull">Pitbull</a>" by Ajax manager <a href="/wiki/Louis_van_Gaal" title="Louis van Gaal">Louis van Gaal</a> due to his fierce style of play in the team's midfield.<sup id="cite_ref-football-oranje.com_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-football-oranje.com-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-One-on-One_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-One-on-One-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Milan_and_Juventus">Milan and Juventus</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Milan and Juventus">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="box-Expand_section plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><a href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg" class="image"><img alt="[icon]" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="14" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="44" data-file-height="31" /></a></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs expansion</b>. <small>You can help by <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">adding to it</a>.</small>  <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">July 2011</span>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Edgar_Davids_(Juventus_F.C.,_no._26)_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_(A.C._Milan)_-_20030528.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg/170px-Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="254" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg/255px-Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bf/Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg/340px-Edgar_Davids_%28Juventus_F.C.%2C_no._26%29_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_%28A.C._Milan%29_-_20030528.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1648" data-file-height="2464" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Edgar_Davids_(Juventus_F.C.,_no._26)_clashing_with_Gennaro_Gattuso_(A.C._Milan)_-_20030528.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>' Davids clashing with <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Gennaro_Gattuso" title="Gennaro Gattuso">Gennaro Gattuso</a> during the final of the <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2002–03 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> on 28 May 2003</div></div></div>
<p>At the start of the <a href="/wiki/1996%E2%80%9397_Serie_A" title="1996–97 Serie A">1996–97 season</a>, Davids moved to Italy to play for Milan. After an unsuccessful spell where he failed to establish himself in the first team, he moved on to league rivals Juventus in December 1997 for a <a href="/wiki/Pound_sterling" title="Pound sterling">£</a>5.3&#160;million <a href="/wiki/Transfer_(association_football)" title="Transfer (association football)">transfer fee</a>. He soon became a permanent first team member in the midfield, usually playing on the left flank or in the centre, as a defensive midfielder, forming a notable midfield parternship alongside French <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmaker</a> <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-One-on-One_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-One-on-One-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Six successful years in <a href="/wiki/Turin" title="Turin">Turin</a> followed, with Davids helping the side to the <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a> title in <a href="/wiki/1997%E2%80%9398_Serie_A" title="1997–98 Serie A">1998</a>, <a href="/wiki/2001%E2%80%9302_Serie_A" title="2001–02 Serie A">2002</a> and <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_Serie_A" title="2002–03 Serie A">2003</a>, as well as two <a href="/wiki/Supercoppa_Italiana" title="Supercoppa Italiana">Supercoppa Italiana</a> and the <a href="/wiki/1999_UEFA_Intertoto_Cup" title="1999 UEFA Intertoto Cup">UEFA Intertoto Cup</a>. Juventus manager <a href="/wiki/Marcello_Lippi" title="Marcello Lippi">Marcello Lippi</a> once described him as "my one-man engine room".<sup id="cite_ref-tuttojuve.com_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tuttojuve.com-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-One-on-One_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-One-on-One-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Davids was often inspirational in Europe, playing 15 times as the club made it all the way to the <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2002–03 UEFA Champions League">2002–03 Champions League</a> final before losing to Milan on <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalties</a>. He had also previously managed to reach the Champions League final with Juventus in <a href="/wiki/1998_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="1998 UEFA Champions League Final">1998</a>, followed by a semi-final finish during the <a href="/wiki/1998%E2%80%9399_UEFA_Champions_League" title="1998–99 UEFA Champions League">1998–99 season</a>, as well as reaching the <a href="/wiki/2002_Coppa_Italia_Final" title="2002 Coppa Italia Final">2002 Coppa Italia Final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-tuttojuve.com_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tuttojuve.com-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="Barcelona_.28loan.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Barcelona_(loan)">Barcelona (loan)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Barcelona (loan)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Davids joined <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> on loan in January 2004 from Juventus. Joining midway through a season where the club was struggling in mid-table and recently appointed manager <a href="/wiki/Frank_Rijkaard" title="Frank Rijkaard">Frank Rijkaard</a> was under considerable pressure, Davids led Barça's successful resurgence of form which saw them finishing second to <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a> in <a href="/wiki/2003%E2%80%9304_La_Liga" title="2003–04 La Liga">La Liga</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Davids' arrival has been cited as the catalyst for the <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">Catalan</a> club's dominance of <a href="/wiki/Football_in_Spain" title="Football in Spain">Spanish</a> and <a href="/wiki/European_football" class="mw-redirect" title="European football">European football</a> during the mid-to-late 2000s (decade), with Barcelona winning <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> the following season (after five years without winning the league title) and a <a href="/wiki/Double_(association_football)#European_Doubles" title="Double (association football)">La Liga and Champions League double</a> in <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_FC_Barcelona_season" title="2005–06 FC Barcelona season">2005–06</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Inter_Milan_and_Tottenham_Hotspur">Inter Milan and Tottenham Hotspur</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Inter Milan and Tottenham Hotspur">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the summer of 2004, Davids permanently moved on to Italian club <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> on a three-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> When Inter terminated the remaining years of his contract in August 2005, he moved to England on a <a href="/wiki/Free_transfer_(association_football)" title="Free transfer (association football)">free transfer</a> to play for <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> He had a successful stay at Tottenham and instantly became a fan favourite. His first and only goal was in a 2–1 away win against <a href="/wiki/Wigan_Athletic_F.C." title="Wigan Athletic F.C.">Wigan Athletic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Davids played for Spurs in the <a href="/wiki/2005%E2%80%9306_FA_Premier_League" title="2005–06 FA Premier League">2005–06</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_FA_Premier_League" title="2006–07 FA Premier League">2006–07</a> seasons, with the club finishing fifth in both seasons.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Ajax">Return to Ajax</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Return to Ajax">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:EdgarDavids_Vermaelen_VdWiel.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/EdgarDavids_Vermaelen_VdWiel.jpg/220px-EdgarDavids_Vermaelen_VdWiel.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/EdgarDavids_Vermaelen_VdWiel.jpg/330px-EdgarDavids_Vermaelen_VdWiel.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/EdgarDavids_Vermaelen_VdWiel.jpg/440px-EdgarDavids_Vermaelen_VdWiel.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:EdgarDavids_Vermaelen_VdWiel.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Davids embraces Ajax team manager <a href="/wiki/David_Endt" title="David Endt">David Endt</a> during his second period at Ajax, with <a href="/wiki/Thomas_Vermaelen" title="Thomas Vermaelen">Thomas Vermaelen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_van_der_Wiel" title="Gregory van der Wiel">Gregory van der Wiel</a> behind.</div></div></div>
<p>Davids signed once more for Ajax on 28 January 2007<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> and played his first match against <a href="/wiki/De_Klassieker" title="De Klassieker">club rivals</a> <a href="/wiki/Feyenoord" title="Feyenoord">Feyenoord</a> on 4 February.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> After the mid-season switch, Davids proved his value for the Ajax team again. He was one of the key <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfielders</a> in the run for the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_Eredivisie" title="2006–07 Eredivisie">Dutch championship</a> that was lost on one single goal to <a href="/wiki/PSV_Eindhoven" title="PSV Eindhoven">PSV</a> on the final day of the league. He also played a major role in Ajax's cup campaign. He secured the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_KNVB_Cup" title="2006–07 KNVB Cup">KNVB Cup</a> for Ajax by scoring the final <a href="/wiki/Penalty_kick_(association_football)" title="Penalty kick (association football)">penalty</a> in a thrilling <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalty shoot-out</a> against <a href="/wiki/AZ_Alkmaar" title="AZ Alkmaar">AZ</a>. Prior to the start of the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Eredivisie" title="2007–08 Eredivisie">2007–08 season</a>, Davids' leg was broken in a pre-season friendly against <a href="/wiki/Go_Ahead_Eagles" title="Go Ahead Eagles">Go Ahead Eagles</a>, sidelining him for around three months.<sup id="cite_ref-Ajax_midfielder_Davids_breaks_leg_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ajax_midfielder_Davids_breaks_leg-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> In May 2008, Davids said he would leave Ajax when his contract expired on 30 June.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Davids played against the <a href="/wiki/LA_Galaxy" title="LA Galaxy">LA Galaxy</a> on 6 December 2008 in an exhibition match held at <a href="/wiki/Mount_Smart_Stadium" title="Mount Smart Stadium">Mount Smart Stadium</a> in <a href="/wiki/Auckland" title="Auckland">Auckland</a>, New Zealand, as part of an Oceania XI All-Star team, despite the fact he is not from Oceania and has never played for an Oceanic club or national team.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Davids was in contract negotiations with English <a href="/wiki/Football_League_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="Football League Championship">Championship</a> club <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> from 22 October 2009,<sup id="cite_ref-Leicester_call_off_Davids_pursuit_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Leicester_call_off_Davids_pursuit-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> however he failed to make a decision for over a week and the club withdrew their offer on 30 October.<sup id="cite_ref-Leicester_call_off_Davids_pursuit_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Leicester_call_off_Davids_pursuit-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crystal_Palace">Crystal Palace</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Crystal Palace">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 20 August 2010, Davids agreed a pay-as-you-play deal with English Championship club <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>. He made his debut on 24 August 2010 at left-back in the Second Round of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Football_League_Cup" title="2010–11 Football League Cup">League Cup</a> against <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth_F.C." title="Portsmouth F.C.">Portsmouth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 8 November 2010, he announced his departure from the club, stating it was "one of the greatest experiences of my life".<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Henrik_Larsson_Euro_2004.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Henrik_Larsson_Euro_2004.jpg/220px-Henrik_Larsson_Euro_2004.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Henrik_Larsson_Euro_2004.jpg/330px-Henrik_Larsson_Euro_2004.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/86/Henrik_Larsson_Euro_2004.jpg/440px-Henrik_Larsson_Euro_2004.jpg 2x" data-file-width="640" data-file-height="480" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Henrik_Larsson_Euro_2004.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Davids <i>(wearing No.8)</i> in the Dutch wall, facing a free kick against <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a> at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2004" title="UEFA Euro 2004">Euro 2004</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>Davids was an integral part of the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_soccer_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Netherlands national soccer team">Netherlands national team</a> since his debut on 20 April 1994 in <a href="/wiki/Tilburg" title="Tilburg">Tilburg</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Republic of Ireland</a> (0–1),<sup id="cite_ref-rsssf.com_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rsssf.com-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> though he has not won any major tournaments for the <i>Oranje</i>.
</p><p>During <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_1996" title="UEFA Euro 1996">UEFA Euro 1996</a>, he was sent home by then manager <a href="/wiki/Guus_Hiddink" title="Guus Hiddink">Guus Hiddink</a> for saying in a radio interview, "Hiddink should stop putting his head in some players' asses."
</p><p>Nonetheless, Davids remained appreciated by Hiddink, who included him in the Dutch squad for the <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998 FIFA World Cup</a> in France. Davids' most notable performance for the national team came in the <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage" title="1998 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">second round</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Serbia_and_Montenegro_national_football_team" title="Serbia and Montenegro national football team">FR Yugoslavia</a>. He scored the winning goal in the last minute of the game and ensured that the Dutch team went through to the next round to meet <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>. The Netherlands eventually finished fourth overall and Davids was named to the official <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> "Team of the Tournament".
</p><p>In 1999, Davids began wearing protective glasses following surgery in his right eye caused by <a href="/wiki/Glaucoma" title="Glaucoma">glaucoma</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> which developed in 1995 following eye injuries. Davids first wore them on 4 September 1999 in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On 17 May 2001, Davids was suspended by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> when he tested positive for the banned <a href="/wiki/Anabolic_steroid" title="Anabolic steroid">anabolic steroid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nandrolone" title="Nandrolone">nandrolone</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Davids played in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2000" title="UEFA Euro 2000">Euro 2000</a> when he was named for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA" title="UEFA">UEFA</a> "Team of the Tournament". The Netherlands reached the semi-finals and played against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_soccer_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Italy national soccer team">Italy</a> in a thrilling game that ended up being decided in Italy's favour with a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Penalty shootout (association football)">penalty shootout</a>.
</p><p>During the Netherlands' <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2004_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2004 qualifying">Euro 2004 qualifying</a> matches, Davids scored the Netherlands' first qualifying goal in their opening 3–0 victory against <a href="/wiki/Belarus_national_football_team" title="Belarus national football team">Belarus</a> and subsequently bossed the midfield in five of the remaining seven Group 3 fixtures and both legs of the play-off victory against <a href="/wiki/Scotland_national_football_team" title="Scotland national football team">Scotland</a>.
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2004" title="UEFA Euro 2004">Euro 2004</a>, new national team coach <a href="/wiki/Marco_van_Basten" title="Marco van Basten">Marco van Basten</a> appointed Davids as captain of the team. However, lack of first team football at his club Inter meant Davids also lost his place in the national team in October 2004, thus losing the captain's armband in the process, which was later handed to goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Edwin_van_der_Sar" title="Edwin van der Sar">Edwin van der Sar</a>. At the latter stages of the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2006 FIFA World Cup qualification">qualifying series</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006 World Cup</a> in October 2005, he was recalled back into the national team, though not as captain. He fell out of the picture again shortly after, thereby missing out on the Dutch squad for the World Cup.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A quick, hard-working, tenacious team player, gifted with power and pace, as well as exceptional physical strength and stamina in spite of his diminutive stature. Davids was renowned for his dynamic and combative style of play, tight marking of opponents, and ability to break down opposition plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defensive_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Defensive midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Defoe_excited_by_Davids_signing_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Defoe_excited_by_Davids_signing-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-tuttojuve.com_8-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tuttojuve.com-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-One-on-One_9-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-One-on-One-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Davids:_Dutch_can_go_all_the_way_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Davids:_Dutch_can_go_all_the_way-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-La_malattia_agli_occhi_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-La_malattia_agli_occhi-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-cult_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cult-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-98_FWC_All-star_team_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98_FWC_All-star_team-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> In addition to his ball-winning ability, as well as his physical and athletic attributes, Davids was also a highly talented and creative player, who was known for his outstanding technique, vision, acceleration, close control, quick footwork, and <a href="/wiki/Keepie_uppie" title="Keepie uppie">ball-juggling skills</a>; his technical ability and prowess at <a href="/wiki/Street_football" title="Street football">street soccer</a> and as a <a href="/wiki/Freestyle_football" title="Freestyle football">freestyle footballer</a> earned him the nickname "The Mayor of the Street" in his youth.<sup id="cite_ref-One-on-One_9-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-One-on-One-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-cult_36-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cult-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Davids was also a powerful striker of the ball, as well as being an accurate passer and crosser with his excellent left foot, which enabled him to create chances for teammates after winning back possession.<sup id="cite_ref-tuttojuve.com_8-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tuttojuve.com-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-La_malattia_agli_occhi_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-La_malattia_agli_occhi-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-cult_36-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cult-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> His tactical intelligence, awareness, and ability to read the game, combined with his speed, energy, tackling, vision, and <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> ability, allowed him to start counter-attacks after winning back possession and also enabled him to make forward attacking runs and contribute to his team's offensive play. His versatility and wide range of skills thus enabled him to be deployed in several other midfield positions throughout his career; he was capable of playing as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">left midfielder</a>, or as a <a href="/wiki/Central_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Central midfielder">central</a> or <a href="/wiki/Box-to-box_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Box-to-box midfielder">box-to-box midfielder</a>, or even as a <a href="/wiki/Left_back" class="mw-redirect" title="Left back">left back</a>, and in his youth, was also deployed as an <a href="/wiki/Attacking_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Attacking midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>, or as a <a href="/wiki/Second_striker" class="mw-redirect" title="Second striker">second striker</a> on occasion.<sup id="cite_ref-football-oranje.com_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-football-oranje.com-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-One-on-One_9-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-One-on-One-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-MasterCard_All-Star_Team_of_the_1998_World_Cup_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MasterCard_All-Star_Team_of_the_1998_World_Cup-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-archive.thedailystar.net_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-archive.thedailystar.net-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Regarded as one of the greatest midfielders of his generation, although he received acclaim for his playing ability and leadership as a footballer, Davids also gained a degree of infamy due to his strong character, temper, and outspokenness, which often led him to be involved in conflicts with his managers; he also struggled with injuries throughout his career.<sup id="cite_ref-football-oranje.com_3-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-football-oranje.com-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-La_malattia_agli_occhi_35-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-La_malattia_agli_occhi-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-cult_36-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cult-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> Due to his aggressive and hard-tackling playing style, Davids earned several nicknames throughout his career, such as "The Piranha", "Tubarão" (The Shark), and most notably, "The Pitbull".<sup id="cite_ref-One-on-One_9-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-One-on-One-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Media">Media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Davids has appeared in commercials for the American sportswear company <a href="/wiki/Nike,_Inc." title="Nike, Inc.">Nike</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Jackson_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jackson-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> In 1996, he starred in a Nike commercial titled "Good vs Evil" in a gladiatorial game set in a <a href="/wiki/Roman_amphitheatre" title="Roman amphitheatre">Roman amphitheatre</a>. Appearing alongside football players from around the world, including <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Maldini" title="Paolo Maldini">Paolo Maldini</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eric_Cantona" title="Eric Cantona">Eric Cantona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Patrick_Kluivert" title="Patrick Kluivert">Patrick Kluivert</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jorge_Campos" title="Jorge Campos">Jorge Campos</a>, they defend "<a href="/wiki/The_Beautiful_Game" title="The Beautiful Game">the beautiful game</a>" against a team of demonic warriors, before it culminates with Cantona striking the ball and destroying evil.<sup id="cite_ref-Jackson_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Jackson-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In a global Nike advertising campaign in the run-up to the <a href="/wiki/2002_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2002 FIFA World Cup">2002 World Cup</a> in Korea and Japan, Davids starred in a "<a href="/wiki/Secret_Tournament" title="Secret Tournament">Secret Tournament</a>" commercial (branded by Nike as "Scorpion KO") directed by <a href="/wiki/Terry_Gilliam" title="Terry Gilliam">Terry Gilliam</a>, appearing alongside football players such as <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronaldinho" title="Ronaldinho">Ronaldinho</a>, <a href="/wiki/Francesco_Totti" title="Francesco Totti">Francesco Totti</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lu%C3%ADs_Figo" title="Luís Figo">Luís Figo</a> and Japanese star <a href="/wiki/Hidetoshi_Nakata" title="Hidetoshi Nakata">Hidetoshi Nakata</a>, with former player Eric Cantona the tournament "referee".<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Davids features in EA Sports' <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i> video game series</a>, and was selected to appear on the cover of <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_Football_2003" title="FIFA Football 2003">FIFA Football 2003</a></i> alongside <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> winger <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Giggs" title="Ryan Giggs">Ryan Giggs</a> and Brazilian international <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Carlos" title="Roberto Carlos">Roberto Carlos</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> The online game <i><a href="/wiki/League_of_Legends" title="League of Legends">League of Legends</a></i> by <a href="/wiki/Riot_Games" title="Riot Games">Riot Games</a> used Davids' likeness for a character skin called Striker Lucian without permission. Davids sued, and Dutch courts ruled that Riot Games must compensate Davids a percentage of their earnings from the skin.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Coaching_career">Coaching career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Coaching career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ajax_2">Ajax</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Ajax">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In June 2011, Davids was elected to the new supervisory board at Ajax alongside <a href="/wiki/Johan_Cruyff" title="Johan Cruyff">Johan Cruyff</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Barnet">Barnet</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Barnet">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Edgar_Davids_16-02-2013_1.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Edgar_Davids_16-02-2013_1.jpg/200px-Edgar_Davids_16-02-2013_1.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="340" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Edgar_Davids_16-02-2013_1.jpg/300px-Edgar_Davids_16-02-2013_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/51/Edgar_Davids_16-02-2013_1.jpg/400px-Edgar_Davids_16-02-2013_1.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1066" data-file-height="1813" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Edgar_Davids_16-02-2013_1.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Davids playing for <a href="/wiki/Barnet_F.C." title="Barnet F.C.">Barnet</a> in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>Since 2010, Davids had been living in <a href="/wiki/North_London" title="North London">North London</a> with his partner and had been participating in street football as well as managing <a href="/wiki/Sunday_league_football" title="Sunday league football">Sunday league</a> amateur side Brixton United.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 11 October 2012, Davids joined <a href="/wiki/Football_League_Two" class="mw-redirect" title="Football League Two">League Two</a> side <a href="/wiki/Barnet_F.C." title="Barnet F.C.">Barnet</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Player-coach" title="Player-coach">player-manager</a> role, alongside <a href="/wiki/Mark_Robson_(footballer)" title="Mark Robson (footballer)">Mark Robson</a>. The next day, on his managerial debut for Barnet, his side lost 4–1 at <a href="/wiki/Underhill_Stadium" title="Underhill Stadium">Underhill</a> to <a href="/wiki/Plymouth_Argyle" class="mw-redirect" title="Plymouth Argyle">Plymouth Argyle</a> which Davids had left himself out of the squad for this <a href="/wiki/Football_League_Two" class="mw-redirect" title="Football League Two">League Two</a> game.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> They followed this up with a 4–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Northampton_Town_F.C." title="Northampton Town F.C.">Northampton Town</a> where Davids played the full match, captaining the team and being voted Man of the Match.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> In November, he started against <a href="/wiki/Morecambe_F.C." title="Morecambe F.C.">Morecambe</a> which Barnet lost 4–1. Near the end of December 2012, following the departure of Robson, Davids took charge of the club by himself.<sup id="cite_ref-Coach_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Coach-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Davids scored his first goal for Barnet in February 2013 in a 2–0 home victory over <a href="/wiki/Southend_United_F.C." title="Southend United F.C.">Southend United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Barnet_2–0_Southend_56-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Barnet_2–0_Southend-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In March 2013, on the return journey from a defeat at <a href="/wiki/Accrington_Stanley_F.C." title="Accrington Stanley F.C.">Accrington Stanley</a>, Davids sent the Barnet team coach back to pick up 36 supporters whose coach had broken down on the motorway and take them to the next service station.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite initially guiding Barnet off the foot of League Two, and lifting them out of the relegation zone, Barnet dropped back into the bottom two on the final day of the 2012–13 season, following a defeat to <a href="/wiki/Northampton_Town_F.C." title="Northampton Town F.C.">Northampton Town</a>, and were relegated out of the <a href="/wiki/Football_League" class="mw-redirect" title="Football League">Football League</a> at the expense of <a href="/wiki/AFC_Wimbledon" title="AFC Wimbledon">AFC Wimbledon</a> who were able to escape by beating <a href="/wiki/Fleetwood_Town_F.C." title="Fleetwood Town F.C.">Fleetwood Town</a>. On 21 May 2013, it was announced that Davids would remain in charge of Barnet for the club's 2013–14 <a href="/wiki/Conference_Premier" class="mw-redirect" title="Conference Premier">Conference Premier</a> season.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> In July 2013, Davids announced his decision to wear the number 1 shirt for the 2013–14 season, a shirt number traditionally worn by <a href="/wiki/Goalkeeper_(association_football)" title="Goalkeeper (association football)">goalkeepers</a>, saying that he intends to "set a trend" of midfielders wearing the number 1 shirt.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Discipline was a major problem for Davids in the 2013–14 season. He was booked in each of the first eight league games he played, and he was sent off three times in those first eight games. There was also controversy when it emerged that he would not attend away games that required an overnight stay, leaving assistant manager <a href="/wiki/Ulrich_Landvreugd" title="Ulrich Landvreugd">Ulrich Landvreugd</a> to take charge.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> In December 2013, Davids considered retiring from football after being sent off for the third time in the season in Barnet's 2–1 defeat by <a href="/wiki/Salisbury_City_F.C." title="Salisbury City F.C.">Salisbury City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Davids resigned from his post as manager on 18 January 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In June 2014, <a href="/wiki/Southern_Counties_East_Football_League" title="Southern Counties East Football League">Southern Counties East Football League</a> side <a href="/wiki/Greenwich_Borough_F.C." title="Greenwich Borough F.C.">Greenwich Borough</a> announced they were "in advanced talks" with Davids, with chairman Perry Skinner stating that he was "70% sure he'll come on board".<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> The following month it was announced the club's attempt to sign Davids had been unsuccessful.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Davids was engaged to fashion designer <a href="/wiki/Olcay_Gulsen" title="Olcay Gulsen">Olcay Gulsen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> In 1999, Davids started his own Street Soccer fashion label called Monta Soccer.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> It offers urban style clothes for men, women, and children around the world. It currently has multiple fashion lines. The Monta Sports,<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> The Monta Studio<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> and Monta Juniors.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Edgar_Davids&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
